# Institution support for Instant Payouts

Identify whether your account's institution supports Instant Payouts.

> Stripe supports Instant Payouts for [eligible users](https://docs.stripe.com/payouts/instant-payouts.md#eligibility-and-daily-volume-limits) in the United States, Canada, the United Kingdom, the European Union, Singapore, Australia, Norway, New Zealand, Malaysia, Hong Kong, and United Arab Emirates. Instant Payouts in each country must use the local currency. For example, an Instant Payout to a Canadian business must be in CAD.

To see which institutions support [Instant Payouts](https://docs.stripe.com/payouts/instant-payouts.md), select your country from the dropdown. Only the listed institutions support Instant Payouts.

#### Instant Payout support in - United States (US)

## Debit cards 

To see which US institutions issue debit cards that can receive Instant Payouts, expand the corresponding section. Values in the Instant Payouts support column indicate whether the institution supports all debit cards or only some debit cards.

See the [European payments council site](https://www.europeanpaymentscouncil.eu/what-we-do/be-involved/register-participants/registers-participants-sepa-payment-schemes) for further details.

#### Instant Payout support in - Other countries

Stripe doesn’t yet support Instant Payouts for users outside Australia, Canada, the European Union, Hong Kong, Malaysia, New Zealand, Norway, Singapore, the United Arab Emirates, the United Kingdom, and the United States. If you’re interested in using Instant Payouts elsewhere, [let us know](https://dashboard.stripe.com/payouts/instant_payouts_eligibility).
